/rgyal ba'i ring bsrel nor bu mchog/
/dgos 'dod thams cad 'byung bar byed/
/nyan thos rang rgyal byang chub sems/
de bzhin mal 'byor ldan pa'i gdung/
/mchod cing lus la bcangs pa yis/
/gdon kun phyogs su nyi mi nus/ /zhes gsungs so/
/rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa'i ring bsrel 'di la brten nas
nor bu gzhan dag kyang 'byung bar bshad pas/ gzhan la'ang byin
rlabs 'byung ba'i rgyu mtshan no/
/slob_dpon klu sgrub kyis/ mi'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin
po che ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ring bsrel las 'byung ste/ dam
pa'i chos nam ma nub kyi bar yul de'i gdul bya skyong la/ dam
pa'i chos nam nub par 'gyur ba'i dus kyi tshe ring bsrel mams
rgya mtsho chen po'i nang du nor bu'i gzugs su 'gyur rol /dper
na lo stong lon pa'i chab rom rin po che spug tu gyur pa bzhin
no/ /zhes gsungs/
sngon sangs rgyas 'jig rten du byon pa mams kyi sku gdung
ring bsrel des sangs rgyas de mya ngan las 'das nas de'i dam
pa'i chos ma nub par de nyid kyis gdul bya skyong zhing/ 'phel
gdung sogs myong na las sgrib byang zhing skye ba dran pa'i mi
lus gtsang ma thob par bshad lal sangs rgyas de'i bstan pa'i
chos nub nas rgya mtsho chen por lhung ste/ nor bu'i rgis su
gyur nas klu'i gdul bya skyong bas na lha klu mi'i nor bu mchog
dman thams cad rgya mtsho rang nas 'byung bas na/ rgya mtsho
la rin chen (p. 77) 'byung gnas zhes pa'i don te/ de'i mchog
mnams ni klu'i lag nas 'byung la) de yang sangs rgyas dang lha
drang srong sogs la klus phul bas sa steng du 'byung ba dang/

yin no/

po che'i rgyal po (f. 15r) 'am rdo'i rgyal po la 'jug/ 'di la
rigs bzhi ste/ basmam gi dang/ ma yũ ram gi dang/ ka chap 61
dang/ bhrum gi'o/
/basmam gi ni ndog sngo la dkar shas che la 'od zer dang
bcas pa'o/
/ma yū ram gi ni/ rma bya'i sgro la rdul gyis cung zad phog
pa 'dra ba'o/
ka gham gi ni sngo nag gi mdog can no/
/bhrum gi ni mdog sngo nag ser kha dang bcas pa'o/
/de ni rgya gar lugs kyi ngos 'azin lugs yin la gang yang
snga ma la gser inga skor sprod cing phyi ma rim pas snga ma'i
bcu sde la gnyis re chag pa'i gong thang byed do/
/bod kyi ngos 'dzin lugs ni/ g.yu rying gsum/ bar g.yu
gnyis/ g.yu gsar gsum dang brgyad du dbye ba yin/ g.yu rying
gsum nið sngo zhing dkar la bkrag mdangs che la mun par yang
mthong ba de la drug dkar dang/ sngo zhing dmar mdangs che la
snum pa drug dmar/ de gnyis zil gyis gnon pa drug dkar las cung
sngo ba la g.yu spyang zer te sman la 'di gsum mchog tu nus pa
che'o/
/bar g.yu gnyis ni/ drug dkar 'dra la de las bkrag chung
zhing 'o kha can gyu sngon/ drug Omar las cung gear la mdangs
zhan pa bar dmar te 'di gnyis nus pa 'bring ba'o/
18.yu gsar ni rigs dbyibs ma nges pa gsar nyams can ni
rgya g.yu ste g.yu ba'u yang zer/ shin tu gsar pa sngon ne 'dra
la rdo sra mkhregs dkar gong 'dra ba 'byar ba'i 'brum pa can g.yu
ro dang/ kha dog zhan pa ser kha dbyibs gsar rnying ma nges pa la
drug se zhes ngan pa'o/
/'di mams ni rgya gar na ye med pas mtsho ma dros pa'i
gting na yod pas/ zla ba bdun pa'i dus char zhod che dus mtsho
dang bod gangs can du 'bab pa'i (p. 80) chu 'brubs pas rkyen
byas nas gangs (f. 15v) can du thor bu 'byung ba dang/ 'ga' zhig
rgya nag dang zhang zhung nas kyang 'byung ngo/



3 varieties
Indra ni la
Shel phreng, f. 16r (p. 81)
/indra ni las nad kun ma lus sel/
/zhes pa 'di la rigs gsum ste/ indra ni la dang/ ni ma la dang/
ka ka ni la'o/
/indra ni la ni/ kha dog sngon po nam mkha' dangs (Lhasa:
dwangs) pa lta bu 'od zer 'bar ba'i steng du ras bzhag na de la
'od kyis phog pa'i 'od zer sngon po gdugs phub pa lta bu steng du
'byung ba che chung sor mo dgu yis 'khyud pa zhig 'byung bar rin
thang nỉ gser stong gỉ skor thang rỉ ggungs so/
Ini ma la ni kha dog snga ma 1ta bu la 'od sor gsum gyi
rgya khyon du sngon por khyab pa che chung sor gsum syi nang du
chud pa tsam zhig 'byung bas gong ni gser brgya skor ri'o/
/ka ka nĩ la ni/ enga ma gnyis las cung zal gnag pa/ nyl
ma gar shar ba'i phyogs su rang gi 'od 'byung la che chung ma
nges pas gong gser bcu skor byed do/
/de gsum ka sing ga la nas yong ba'i chu bo bzhi'i nang gi
chu bo dharma ganggā zhes bya ba'i nang nas 'byung ba'o/



3 varieties
Bai dū rya

/nor bu rin chen bai dū rya'i rigs kyi/
l'od dang 'chang bas nad kun sel bar byed/

nu bai dū rya/ manydzu ni bai dù rya'o/

na 'od zer 'byung bas mun pa 'phrog pa nang du skud pa gsum bcug
pa 'dra ba zhig yod pas/ rin thang yul sde che ba zhig ri bar
bshad do/
la nu bai dū rya ni/ 'od zer med pa mdog dkar po nang du
skud pa gcig bcug pa 'dra ba zhig yod pas rin thang yul phran
gcig ri bar gsungs so/
/manydzu ni bai dū rya ni byi la'i mig ltar ser ba/ (p. 81)
mtshan mo 'od zer 'byung ba nang du skud pa dgu bcug pa 'dra ba
(f. 16r) me la bcug na 'od zer lhag par che ba'o/ /rin thang ni
gling bzhi ka'i sde zog ri zhes bshad tshad du 'dug go/
/'di la rie rang byung rdo ries/
byi la'i mig 'dras sbrul chen srung/ /zhes gsungs/

bar bstan bcos las bshad kyang/ deng sang phal cher singga la'i

9 varieties
Padma rā ga
Shel phreng, ff. 16v-17r (pp. 82-83)
/padma rā gas nad dang gdon kun 'phrog/
/ces pa ni/ padma rā ga'am/ padma rakta zhes padma dmar po ste/
'di la rigs dgu yod pa ni/ padma rakta dang/ puşpa rakta dang/
dza ti rā ga dang/ lla la rā ga (Lhasa: lla la ra ga) dang/ mu
la rangga rakta dang/ ha ri gau ri dang/ pug dang/ bi dza ya dang/
gau mo da dang dgu'o/
/padma rakta ni mdog ngur dmar rang 'od kyis sor gsum du
khyab pa/ mtheb mdzub kyis 'dus pa'i tshad tsam yod do/
/puşpa (Lhasa: puşpe) rakta ni/ mdog dmar smug kha dog gcig
las 'od zer rang las bdun 'gyur tsam pa gsum 'byung ba che tshad
mtheb mdzub kyis 'dus pa tsam mo/
/dza ti rā ga (Lhasa: dza ti rwa ga) ni/ sprin dmar mched
pa'i mdog can 'od khru gang tsam gyi tshad tsam du nar mor 'gro
ba che tshad kyang tsu ta'i 'bru tsam zhig 'byung ngo/
/lla la rā ga ni/ kha dog sol ba la me mched pa 'dra ba 'od
aor gsum tsan phyogs gcig kho nar 'byung ba che chung mtheb skor
mos tshud pa tsam 'byung ngo/
/mu la ram ga rakta ni, se 'bru'i 'bras bu shin tu smin
pa'i mdog can/ 'od kyang khrag gi mdog tu 'byung ba che chung
mtheb chen tsam 'byung ngo/
la ri gau ri ni/ gos chen dmar smug shin tu dwangs pa'i
mdog can bsgyur ba na 'od dmar po dang ser po gnyis ka 'byung
ba che tshad sran ma 'phos pa tsam 'byung ngo/
/pug (p. 82) ni/ mdog rab tu dmar ba 'od (f. 16v) zer ser po
sor do'i tshad tsam phyogs gcig tu 'gro ba che tahad mtheb mdzub
gnyis kyi rtses 'dus pa tsam mo/
. /bi dza ya ni/ me'i mdog can od zer sor gang gi tshad tsam
phyogs gcig tu 'gro ba che tshad se 'bru'i 'bras bu tsam mo/
/gau mo da (Lhasa: go mo da) ni/ phyi mchin kha la nang me
Ita bu sa la bzhag na 'od mi 'byung la mkha' la bteg na 'od 'byung
ba che chung tshad nges pa med pa'o /
/de rnams ni gtso bo sing ga la nas 'byung/ pug ni ham sa
wa ti nas 'byung/ gong thang gi tshad nỉ bzang shot dang/ ha rị
gau ri lal glang po che'i steng nas rde'u tshag 'phen gyis bskyur
ba sa la phog tshun thang mar gdal ba'i tshad kyi gser ri zhes
gong med pa'i tshad du bshad pa'o/

Ba ru ra
Ray, p. 55
vibhitaka
Syn.: akşa, vibhitaki, tusā, vibhita, kāmaghna
Beleric myrobalan (Terminalia belerica Retz.)
The dried fruits used alone or in prescriptions (internal)
Cough, heart-disease, etc.; as purgative and blood-cleanser
Chopra, p. 241
TERMINALIA (Combretaceae)
Terminalia belerica Roxb.
S. Bahira
H., P., B. Bahera
Bo. Behara
Tam. Akkam
Tel. Tandra
Mal. Tusham
M. Tandi
Assam. Hulluch
Fruit -- bitter, astrin., tonic, laxt., antipyr., used in piles,
dropsy, diar., leprosy, biliousness, dyspep. and headache;
when half ripe purg., when fully ripe astrin.
Kernel -- narcotic



Skyu ru ra
Ray, p. 52
āmalaki
Syn.: dhātrī, kāyasthā, amoghā, āmalaka
Emblic myrobolan (Phyllanthus emblica Linn.)
The dried fruit or the fresh juice used in prescriptions
(internal)
As a tonic in a very large number of diseases
Chopra, p. 106
EMBLICA (Euphorbiaceae)
Emblica officinalis Gaertn. (syn. Phyllanthus emblica Linn.)
B. Amla, Amlaki
H. Amla, Aonla
Kan. Amalaka
Mal. Nelli
S. Adiphala, Amalaka
Tam. Nelli
Tel. Amalakamu
Fruit -- acrid, cooling, refrig., diur., laxt.
Raw fruit -- aper
Dried fruit -- useful in haemor., diar., and dysen.; in combination
with iron used for anaemia, jaundice and dyspep.
Fermented liquor prepared from the fruit -- used in jaundice, dyspep.
and cough
Sherbet of amla with lemon juice -- taken for arresting acute bacillary
dysen.
Exudation from incisions on the fruit used as external apprication for
the inflam of the eye
Flowers -- cooling, refrig., aper.
Root and bark -- astrin.
Seeds -- used for asthma, broncht. and biliousness

Na le sham
na le sham
pho ba ris
pho tshe
drod sman hril mo
VARIETIES
1. nag po - probably to be identified with black pepper (Piper
nigrum Linn.)
2. dkar po - probably the sveta marica or "white pepper" about
which there is some controversy. The sveta marica
found in the bazar is usually black pepper which
has been peeled before grinding. Some ayurvedic
practitioners however identify sveta marica with
the seed of the drum-stick plant (Moringa pterygo-
spermus Gaertn.)
sba tsha -- Das: the residue of mustard seed after oil has
been pressed out
skabs sbyar gtong -- ? to be used as the occasion requires
skabs dang sbyar ba - fit for, adapted, suited to the occasion



Na le sham
Ray, p. 66
marica
Syn.: --
Black pepper plant (Piper nigrum Linn.)
The dried seeds used as spice or in prescriptions (internal)
Rhinitis, anaemia, fainting, consumption, cough, etc.
Chopra, p. 194
PIPER (Piperaceae)
Piper nigrum Linn.
S. Maricha
Tam. Milagu
Mal. Kurumulaka
Tel. Marichamu
H. Golmirch
B. Golmorich
Bo. Kala miri
Fruit -- used as arom. stim. in cholera, in weakness following
fevers, vertigo, coma; as stomch. in dyspep. and flatulence;
as antiper. in malarial fever; as an alter. in paraplegia
and arthritic diseases; externally used as rubft. and as
a local application for relaxed sore-throat, piles and
skin diseases.
Ray, p. 73
sigra
Syn.: sobhāñjana, sigru, haritaśāka, raktaka
Drum-stick plant (Moringa pterygospermus Gaertn.)
The powdered bark, root, and dried sap used in prescriptions of
in steaming mixtures (internal and external)
Anosmia, fainting, chronic skin eruptions, painful piles, etc.
Chopra, p. 170
MORINGA (Moringaceae)
Moringa oleifera Lam. (Syn. M. pterygosperma Gaertn.)
S. Sobhanjana
H., P. Soanjna
B. Sajna
Bo. Sujna
Tam. Murungai
Tel. Sajana
Mal. Sigru
Seeds -- used in venereal affections

pippali

Long-pepper plant (Piper longum Linn.)
The dried flowers, fruits, and roots used as ingredients of
prescriptions; also as a spice in cooking

PIPER (Piperaceae)

S. Pippali
P., H., B., and Bo.: Piplamul
Mal. Pippali
Tel. Pippallu
Dried unripe fruit -- alter. tonic
Decoct. of immature fruit and root -- used in chronic broncht.,
cough, and cold
Root and fruit -- antid. to snake-bite and scorpion-sting

Byi tang ga
Ray, p. 77
vidanga
Syn.: bhasmaka, ghoşā, citrabijā
Embelia plant (Embelia ribes Burm.f.)
Used as dried powder, or the decoction in prescriptions (ex-
ternal and internal)
Chronic skin diseases, dysentery, diarrhoea, etc.: for oral
hygiene, and as purgative
Chopra, p. 106
EMBELIA (Myrsinaceae)
Embelia ribes Burm. f.
S. Vidanga
P. Babrung
H. Baberang
B. Biranga
Bo. Vaivarang, Vavadinga
Tam., Tel., and Kan. Vayuvilanga
Dried fruit -- antihelm., astrin., alter., tonic, in scorpion-sting,
S and snake-bite
Decoct. of dried fruits -- used for fevers and diseases of chest
and skin
Infusion of roots -- given for coughs and diar.

Shing sman me tog
Shel phreng, pp. 216-219
/gayis pa shing sman me tog nus pa bshad pa ni/.../zhes shing
sman me tog gi rigs rtsa ba drug dang nang tshan bzhi bcas rgyas

/nā ga puşpa nā ga ge sar dang/
rtsa ba: puspe
/padma ge sar glo mchin snying tshad sel/
/da lis bad ken grang sel tshe bcud len/
/spen dkar so rtsi nag pos nu tshab sel/
/stag mai me tog Myang khog rang skem mahog/
/se ba'i me tog mkhris sel rlung kha gnon/
/skyer pa'i me tog 'bras bu 'khru ba gcod/
I. Nā-ga-ge-sar
A. Varieties: 0
Sone authorities reckon that there are three varieties;
others only two; author holds that it is an identical plant.
1. Ge sar sum ldan
a. Phyi Padma ge sar
b. Nang Na ga ge sar
c. Bar Utpal ge sar
2. Another way of reckoning:
a. Nā-ga-puşpa
b. Na-ga-ge-sar or Utpal-ge-sar
C. Padma-ge-sar
3. Most Tibetan physicians reckon only two varieties:
a. Padma-ge-sar
b. Nå-ga-ge-sar
B. Names:
1. Tsam-se-ya
2. Ke-sar
3. Na-ga-ke-sar (Klu'i-ge-sar)
4. Ge-sar-can
5. Känytsa-ra-na-ha-la (Gser-ming-can)
6. Ke-sar
(Ge-sar or Padma'i-skra or Ze-ba or Ze-'bru)
7. Nā-ga-puspa (Klu'i-me-tog).

rang byung pas/

/bcud len dri med tshad rkyang sel/ /zhes pa la/
rigs dkar ser dmar smug bzhi yod/

pa ti kam/ gos can rnams zer la/

khanda/ dpal gyi dum bu/ shwe ta tsanda na dang) shukla tsanda na/

sar zer
DKAR PO 'di la rigs gsum yod par bshad del 'grel pa las/
til mar 'dab can zhes bya ba'i tsandan dang/
go shirsa zhes pa mchog gam ba lang mgo zhes bya ba ste/
dbyibs ba lang mgo'i rnam pa can te/ 'di gnyis ma la ya'i ri las
skyes pa dang/

./kha cig ni go shirşa lha yul na yod pa dang/ sbrul gyi

sgrub la klus phul ba cung zad las med ces bshad na yang/ yod pa'i
rgyu mtshan yang bshad yod pa ni/ sngon chos rgyal srong btsan
sgam pos thugs dam gyi rten gdan 'dren pa'i phyir smin (f. 86r)
mtshams nas sprul pa'i dge slong a kar ma ti zhes bya ba sangs
rgyas 'od dpag (p. 221) med dbu la bzhugs pa zhig nam mkhar 'phur
nas 'phags yul du phebs pas/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig gis rab
tu gnas par mdzad pa'i mchod rten padma'i 'khor lo can gyi bum

pho brang du spyan drangs tshe zhal gyis ma bzhes par) yang gsol

ba btab bka' ci bsgos bsgrub par rgyal pos dam bcas pas/ pho brang

bzhengs pa'i nang rten du tsandan go shirga dang/ sbrul snying
las grub pa'i thugs rje chen po'i sku re bzhugs su gsol gsungs pas/

de gnyis len pa'i phyir/ 'khor bcas si ga la'i rgya mtsho'i 'gram

222) pa (Lhasa: ba) bzhin glang po che mams bskrog nas de'i 'og
gi bye ma brkos so/

'dug pas/ rgyal po ngo mtshar nas/ dge slong la mi yul du med pa'i
tsandan 'di ji ltar byung/ de glang po ches ji ltar shes dris pas/

pa'i dus su/ dgra bcom pa zhig rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkhar 'phur
bas/ sum cu rtsa gsum du byon nas tsandan gyi gang bu zhig khyer
nas byon pa'i nang du 'bras bu bzhi 'dug pa gsum sangs rgyas 'khor
ba 'jig la phul cig jo bo kharsa pā şi la phul nas dbu thog tu
bzhag pas/ rlung gis sku rgyab tu 'phangs pa sa la lhung ba/ sas

Tsandan dkar po
thim ma thag dal bus chod cig ces pa'i rang sgra byung ba bzhin
bcad nas tshal pa bzhir gshags (Lhasa: bshags) pa'i nang gi
snying po la/ 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal rang byon byung/ de'i thugs
ga'i 'od rgya bal gyi mtshams su 'phros pa der dge slong byon pas
(f. 87r) nags khrod zhig tu ha ri tsandan gyi sdong po chen po
od zer 'phro ba zhig la/ las dang skal bar idan (p. 223) pa'i
ma he zhig gis bskor ba byed cing nu zhos mchod pa 'thor ba zhig
'dug pas/ tsandan deli nang du jo bo mched bzhi rang byon bzhugs
pa mkhan (Lhasa: mkhyen) nas/ de gcod par brtsams tshe stod nas
rim pas dal bus chod la jo bo rams gnas 'di dang 'dir bzhugs
shig ces pa'i sgra byung ba bzhin gshags pa'i nang nas jo bo
mched bzhi byon pa'i/ 'phags pa wa ti mang yul du bzhugs pas yul
de'i rims kyi 'jigs pa zhi/ 'phags pa dbu gang grong khyer yumbu
glang mkhar du bzhugs pas yul de'i nad kyi 'jigs pa zhi/ 'phags
pa rgya ma li rgya bal mtshams su bzhugs pas yul der steng gdon
gyi 'jigs pa zhi/ 'phags pa lo ke shwa ra po ta lar bzhugs pa
rgyal po'i thugs dam gyi rten mdzad/ da lta bcu gcig zhal gyi
thugs kar bzhugs/
yang sprul pa'i dge slong des kasthu ri'i dri mas sbril
rengs par mdzad de/ ma la ya nas sbrul gyi snying po blangs te
'phags pa'i sku brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs/ des na tsandan dkon
pa mnams rgya gar du yod pa dang/ de'i shing tshal pa rnams gtsug
lag khang gỉ shing byas pas bzos pa'i rat mo dang/ da lta dus
ngan tshe gtsug lag phal cher mu stegs pas bshig pa'i shing cha
bcas/ da lta'i skabs 'dir je jer mod pa'i rgyu mtshan yin no/
/lar shin tu bazang ba 'khrul med mda' snyug team re mar khu
khol ma'i nang du btsugs pas mar khu 'khyags pa de yin yang shin
tu dkon/
'dra yig dung gi mig las/
tsandan dkar po dag la rigs gsum yod/
/sbrul gyi snying po dkar yol bcag pa 'dra/
/go shirşa ni stag ma bcag pa 'dra/
sa mchog som ste som pa'i dum bu 'dra/
/kun kyang snum la dri zhim bzang/ /zhes (f. 87v) dang/
brda sprod pa las/
tsandan bzang ngan chu la dris/
/chur (p. 224) byings (Lhasa: bying) ngad pa ldan pa bzang/
/zhes gsungs/ da lta dkar po mkhregs pa zhig dang/ cung zad ser
kha yod pa zhig/ dmar la shing sna gsal ba zhig dang gsum sogs/
snga ma shing sna thung ba ste/ de dag la snum tshi (Lhasa: tshil)

Dbyi mong

/nyin srib gnyis ka dag las skye/

Igrang ba drung 'byin mkhris pa skye/
/gnyis ka rgas nas mi rgan 'ara/
/grang skran 'dul ba'i dar ya kan/
/ro ni tsha la yid tsam mngar/

/skran rigs 'dul la chu ser 'dren/ /zhes rigs gnyis gsungs
kyang/ gsum du byed pa yin tel
dkar po me tog dkar chung dril bu lta bus grang ba sel zhing
tsha ba mi skye/

Glang ma

Tshi ba thang chu
Shel phreng, pp. 241-245

te drug pa'o/

/tshi ba thang chu'i nus pa bstan pa ni/

chad) dang/

/nags ma'i thang chus mag 'bigs chu ser 'dzin/
/rgya skyegs 'gram 'khrugs khrug nad tshad pa sel/ (Shel phreng reads:
'grem, probably incorrectly)
/la chas (Shel phreng: kşas) glo mkhal 'gram tshad sel ba yin/
/mon (Shel phreng: man) cha ra yis tsha grang 'khru ba gcod/
/thang khrag sa dug 'khru nad sel bar byed/

*/zhes dri med shel gyi phreng ba las bar gyi Inga pa de
